  <tbody class="d-block">
    <tr class="d-block">
      <td class="d-block comment-body markdown-body  js-comment-body">
          <p><a href="https://github.com/nextcloud/ios-communication-library/blob/3abaa65cf70f7dfa8a7d0df2277d4eda14d7cfd1/NCCommunication/NCCommunicationModel.swift#L529">https://github.com/nextcloud/ios-communication-library/blob/3abaa65cf70f7dfa8a7d0df2277d4eda14d7cfd1/NCCommunication/NCCommunicationModel.swift#L529</a></p>
<p>but I use different query :</p>
<p>1 for detect the news images (from #now to first date image)<br>
2 for detect new images in the period from the first visible image to last visible image<br>
3 for detect old images with a recursive called:</p>
<ul>
<li>start search last data -30 gg</li>
<li>if not find search last data -90 gg</li>
<li>if not find search last data -180 gg</li>
<li>if not find search last data distantPast</li>
</ul>
<p>with a limit of 300 items.</p>
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr class="d-block">
      <td class="d-block comment-body markdown-body  js-comment-body">
          <p>Looping in <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skjnldsv/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skjnldsv">@skjnldsv</a><br>
It seems that this query is fast enough: 5-10s on first query:</p>
<pre><code>&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?&gt;
&lt;d:searchrequest xmlns:d="DAV:" xmlns:oc="http://nextcloud.com/ns"&gt;
    &lt;d:basicsearch&gt;
        &lt;d:select&gt;
            &lt;d:prop&gt;
                &lt;d:getcontenttype/&gt;
                &lt;d:resourcetype/&gt;
                &lt;d:getcontentlength/&gt;
                &lt;d:getlastmodified/&gt;
                &lt;d:getetag/&gt;
                &lt;oc:permissions xmlns:oc="http://owncloud.org/ns"/&gt;
                &lt;oc:id xmlns:oc="http://owncloud.org/ns"/&gt;
                &lt;oc:size xmlns:oc="http://owncloud.org/ns"/&gt;
                &lt;oc:favorite xmlns:oc="http://owncloud.org/ns"/&gt;
            &lt;/d:prop&gt;
        &lt;/d:select&gt;
        &lt;d:from&gt;
            &lt;d:scope&gt;
                &lt;d:href&gt;/files/{{ username  }}&lt;/d:href&gt;
                &lt;d:depth&gt;infinity&lt;/d:depth&gt;
            &lt;/d:scope&gt;
        &lt;/d:from&gt;
        &lt;d:where&gt;
					&lt;d:and&gt;
						&lt;d:or&gt;
            &lt;d:like&gt;&lt;d:prop&gt;&lt;d:getcontenttype/&gt;&lt;/d:prop&gt;&lt;d:literal&gt;image/%&lt;/d:literal&gt;&lt;/d:like&gt;
							&lt;d:like&gt;&lt;d:prop&gt;&lt;d:getcontenttype/&gt;&lt;/d:prop&gt;&lt;d:literal&gt;video/%&lt;/d:literal&gt;&lt;/d:like&gt;
						&lt;/d:or&gt;
						&lt;d:gt&gt;&lt;d:prop&gt;&lt;d:getlastmodified/&gt;&lt;/d:prop&gt;&lt;d:literal&gt;1604994646&lt;/d:literal&gt;&lt;/d:gt&gt;
						&lt;/d:and&gt;
        &lt;/d:where&gt;
        &lt;d:orderby&gt;
            &lt;d:order&gt;
                &lt;d:prop&gt;
                    &lt;d:getlastmodified/&gt;
                &lt;/d:prop&gt;
                &lt;d:descending/&gt;
            &lt;/d:order&gt;
        &lt;/d:orderby&gt;
        &lt;d:limit&gt;
            &lt;d:nresults&gt;10&lt;/d:nresults&gt;
        &lt;/d:limit&gt;
    &lt;/d:basicsearch&gt;
&lt;/d:searchrequest&gt;
</code></pre>
<p>This searches for any image/video type, but only for files which were modified in last 10 days.</p>
<p>Next query could then be 10-20 days ago, as <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/marinofaggiana/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/marinofaggiana">@marinofaggiana</a> suggests.</p>
<p>What do you think?</p>
      </td>

      <td class="d-block comment-body markdown-body  js-comment-body">
          <blockquote>
<p>Tested now after a clear cache for c.nc.c practically instant for 300 items</p>
</blockquote>
<p>I also fail to understand why "almost instant" is possible on iOS for 300 items and <strong>including</strong> shared files</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Looping in <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/skjnldsv/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/skjnldsv">@skjnldsv</a><br>
It seems that this query is fast enough: 5-10s on first query:</p>
</blockquote>
<p>but for the Android user experience, 5-10 seconds is good enough with less items and shared files have to be excluded.</p>
<p>What makes it technically impossible to have the same instant user experience on Android, including shared files?</p>
<p>Why does the product owner of the Android app accept that the media tab is broken for that long? Not only in terms of speed but also in terms of usability, i.e. not loading all images and not showing the latest images first without any possibility to navigate. The latter two are even regressions.</p>
<p>Please remove the commits that introduced the change from the photos to the media tab if it is not possible to fix the media tab in the short term. The photos tab was slow it did fail but, as sad as that might sound given its performance, it did work a lot better than the current media tab.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>seems like Nextcloud dose not seem to focus too hard on Android platform and focuses more on the IOS platform I hope there can be a resolution to this soon.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Either no one within the nextcloud team is using the Android app or those that do, do not use the photos/media tab. Otherwise I cannot explain how it can happen that it is so slow compared to iOS and now even completely broken. Adding to that, the iOS/Android devs do not seem to communicate and compare their apps' UX and functionality regularly. Neither does there seem to be a product owner that takes over that job for them and sets priorities for the sprint planning in order to achieve that goal.</p>
      </td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>
